Flushes any cached drawing operations.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Context} & is a pointer to the drawing context to use.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function flushes any cached drawing operations. For display drivers that draw into a local frame buffer before writing to the actual display, calling this function will cause the display to be updated to match the contents of the local frame buffer.

\index{Primitives\+\_\+api@{Primitives\+\_\+api}!Gr\+Font\+Baseline\+Get@{Gr\+Font\+Baseline\+Get}}
\index{Gr\+Font\+Baseline\+Get@{Gr\+Font\+Baseline\+Get}!Primitives\+\_\+api@{Primitives\+\_\+api}}
\paragraph[{Gr\+Font\+Baseline\+Get}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define Gr\+Font\+Baseline\+Get(
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{}]{p\+Font}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)~((p\+Font)-\/$>$uc\+Baseline)}\label{group__primitives__api_gac2b082feb5f30948dbbc06edabc5cdcf}
Gets the baseline of a font.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Font} & is a pointer to the font to query.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function determines the baseline position of a font. The baseline is the offset between the top of the font and the bottom of the capital letters. The only font data that exists below the baseline are the descenders on some lower-\/case letters (such as ``y\textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}).

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns the baseline of the font, in pixels. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\index{Primitives\+\_\+api@{Primitives\+\_\+api}!Gr\+Font\+Height\+Get@{Gr\+Font\+Height\+Get}}
\index{Gr\+Font\+Height\+Get@{Gr\+Font\+Height\+Get}!Primitives\+\_\+api@{Primitives\+\_\+api}}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{}]{p\+Font}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)~((p\+Font)-\/$>$uc\+Height)}\label{group__primitives__api_gabf5ee1d9a55f4b4e5afea07eb0a160b0}
Gets the height of a font.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Font} & is a pointer to the font to query.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function determines the height of a font. The height is the offset between the top of the font and the bottom of the font, including any ascenders and descenders.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns the height of the font, in pixels. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{Primitives\+\_\+api@{Primitives\+\_\+api}!Gr\+Image\+Colors\+Get@{Gr\+Image\+Colors\+Get}}

Gets the number of colors in an image.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Image} & is a \hyperlink{structt_image}{t\+Image} struct\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function determines the number of colors in the palette of an image. This is only valid for 4bpp and 8bpp images; 1bpp images do not contain a palette.

\index{Primitives\+\_\+api@{Primitives\+\_\+api}!Gr\+String\+Baseline\+Get@{Gr\+String\+Baseline\+Get}}
\index{Gr\+String\+Baseline\+Get@{Gr\+String\+Baseline\+Get}!Primitives\+\_\+api@{Primitives\+\_\+api}}
\paragraph[{Gr\+String\+Baseline\+Get}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define Gr\+String\+Baseline\+Get(
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{}]{p\+Context}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)~((p\+Context)-\/$>$p\+Font-\/$>$uc\+Baseline)}\label{group__primitives__api_ga1a557c1a7517cdc1e61e5728ee3969ff}
Gets the baseline of a string.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Context} & is a pointer to the drawing context to query.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function determines the baseline position of a string. The baseline is the offset between the top of the string and the bottom of the capital letters. The only string data that exists below the baseline are the descenders on some lower-\/case letters (such as ``y\textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}).

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns the baseline of the string, in pixels. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\index{Primitives\+\_\+api@{Primitives\+\_\+api}!Gr\+String\+Draw\+Centered@{Gr\+String\+Draw\+Centered}}
\index{Gr\+String\+Draw\+Centered@{Gr\+String\+Draw\+Centered}!Primitives\+\_\+api@{Primitives\+\_\+api}}
\paragraph[{Gr\+String\+Draw\+Centered}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define Gr\+String\+Draw\+Centered(
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{}]{p\+Context, }
\item[{}]{pc\+String, }
\item[{}]{l\+Length, }
\item[{}]{l\+X, }
\item[{}]{l\+Y, }
\item[{}]{b\+Opaque}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\label{group__primitives__api_ga4ab68eecbbfcca392b8d4642b681d912}
{\bfseries Value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}
\textcolor{keywordflow}{do}                                                                  \(\backslash\)
        \{                                                                   \(\backslash\)
            const tContext *pC = pContext;                                  \(\backslash\)
            const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *pcStr = pcString;                                   \
                                                                            \
            GrStringDraw(pC, pcStr, lLength,                                \(\backslash\)
                         (lX) - (GrStringWidthGet(pC, pcStr, lLength) / 2), \(\backslash\)
                         (lY) - (pC->pFont->ucBaseline / 2), bOpaque);      \(\backslash\)
        \}                                                                   \(\backslash\)
        while(0)
\end{DoxyCode}
Draws a centered string.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Context} & is a pointer to the drawing context to use. \\
\hline
{\em pc\+String} & is a pointer to the string to be drawn. \\
\hline
{\em l\+Length} & is the number of characters from the string that should be drawn on the screen. \\
\hline
{\em l\+X} & is the X coordinate of the center of the string position on the screen. \\
\hline
{\em l\+Y} & is the Y coordinate of the center of the string position on the screen. \\
\hline
{\em b\+Opaque} & is {\bfseries true} if the background of each character should be drawn and {\bfseries false} if it should not (leaving the background as is).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function draws a string of test on the screen centered upon the provided position. The {\itshape l\+Length} parameter allows a portion of the string to be examined without having to insert a N\+U\+L\+L character at the stopping point (which would not be possible if the string was located in flash); specifying a length of -\/1 will cause the entire string to be rendered (subject to clipping).

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\index{Primitives\+\_\+api@{Primitives\+\_\+api}!Gr\+String\+Height\+Get@{Gr\+String\+Height\+Get}}
\index{Gr\+String\+Height\+Get@{Gr\+String\+Height\+Get}!Primitives\+\_\+api@{Primitives\+\_\+api}}
\paragraph[{Gr\+String\+Height\+Get}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define Gr\+String\+Height\+Get(
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{}]{p\+Context}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)~((p\+Context)-\/$>$p\+Font-\/$>$uc\+Height)}\label{group__primitives__api_ga258ddad68eadf9d1c03d1c0a97d3e215}
Gets the height of a string.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Context} & is a pointer to the drawing context to query.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function determines the height of a string. The height is the offset between the top of the string and the bottom of the string, including any ascenders and descenders. Note that this will not account for the case where the string in question does not have any characters that use descenders but the font in the drawing context does contain characters with descenders.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns the height of the string, in pixels. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\index{Primitives\+\_\+api@{Primitives\+\_\+api}!Gr\+String\+Max\+Width\+Get@{Gr\+String\+Max\+Width\+Get}}
\index{Gr\+String\+Max\+Width\+Get@{Gr\+String\+Max\+Width\+Get}!Primitives\+\_\+api@{Primitives\+\_\+api}}
\paragraph[{Gr\+String\+Max\+Width\+Get}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define Gr\+String\+Max\+Width\+Get(
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{}]{p\+Context}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)~((p\+Context)-\/$>$p\+Font-\/$>$uc\+Max\+Width)}\label{group__primitives__api_gaca6b9b536d4b4584561e132de35db9f2}
Gets the maximum width of a character in a string.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Context} & is a pointer to the drawing context to query.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function determines the maximum width of a character in a string. The maximum width is the width of the widest individual character in the font used to render the string, which may be wider than the widest character that is used to render a particular string.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns the maximum width of a character in a string, in pixels. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{Primitives\+\_\+api@{Primitives\+\_\+api}!Dpy\+Color\+Translate@{Dpy\+Color\+Translate}}
\index{Dpy\+Color\+Translate@{Dpy\+Color\+Translate}!Primitives\+\_\+api@{Primitives\+\_\+api}}
\paragraph[{Dpy\+Color\+Translate}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define Dpy\+Color\+Translate(
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{}]{p\+Display, }
\item[{}]{ul\+Value}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)~((p\+Display)-\/$>$p\+Fxns-\/$>$pfn\+Color\+Translate((p\+Display)-\/$>$pv\+Display\+Data, ul\+Value))}\label{group__primitives__api_ga49a5dcca6ebf8e21292437f51803166f}
Translates a 24-\/bit R\+G\+B color to a display driver-\/specific color.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Display} & is the pointer to the display driver structure for the display to operate upon. \\
\hline
{\em ul\+Value} & is the 24-\/bit R\+G\+B color. The least-\/significant byte is the blue channel, the next byte is the green channel, and the third byte is the red channel.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function translates a 24-\/bit R\+G\+B color into a value that can be written into the display\textquotesingle{}s frame buffer in order to reproduce that color, or the closest possible approximation of that color.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns the display-\/driver specific color. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\bfseries Value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}
\textcolor{keywordflow}{do}                                                                   \(\backslash\)
        \{                                                                    \
            tDisplay *pD = pDisplay;                                   \(\backslash\)
            pD->pFxns->pfnPixelDrawMultiple(pD, lX, lY, lX0, lCount, \(\backslash\)
                                     lBPP, pucData, pucPalette);             \(\backslash\)
        \}                                                                    \(\backslash\)
        while(0)
\end{DoxyCode}
Draws a horizontal sequence of pixels on a display.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Display} & is the pointer to the display driver structure for the display to operate upon. \\
\hline
{\em l\+X} & is the X coordinate of the first pixel. \\
\hline
{\em l\+Y} & is the Y coordinate of the first pixel. \\
\hline
{\em l\+X0} & is sub-\/pixel offset within the pixel data, which is valid for 1 or 4 bit per pixel formats. \\
\hline
{\em l\+Count} & is the number of pixels to draw. \\
\hline
{\em l\+B\+P\+P} & is the number of bits per pixel; must be 1, 4, or 8. \\
\hline
{\em puc\+Data} & is a pointer to the pixel data. For 1 and 4 bit per pixel formats, the most significant bit(s) represent the left-\/most pixel. \\
\hline
{\em puc\+Palette} & is a pointer to the palette used to draw the pixels.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function draws a horizontal sequence of pixels on a display, using the supplied palette. For 1 bit per pixel format, the palette contains pre-\/translated colors; for 4 and 8 bit per pixel formats, the palette contains 24-\/bit R\+G\+B values that must be translated before being written to the display.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Fills a rectangle on a display.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Display} & is the pointer to the display driver structure for the display to operate upon. \\
\hline
{\em p\+Rect} & is a pointer to the structure describing the rectangle to fill. \\
\hline
{\em ul\+Value} & is the color to fill the rectangle.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function fills a rectangle on the display. This assumes that clipping has already been performed, and that all sides of the rectangle are within the extents of the display.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Determines if a point lies within a given rectangle.

\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}
